#COUP DEBUG#

country_event = { #sogno and borghese debug
	id = coupdebug.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event coupdebug.1" }
	title = coupdebug.1.t
	desc = coupdebug.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_right_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #sogno coup
		name = coupdebug.1.a
		ITA_army_add_sogno_pop = yes
		ITA_navy_add_sogno_pop = yes
		ITA_airforce_add_sogno_pop = yes
		ITA_carabinieri_add_sogno_pop = yes
		set_global_flag = ITA_lost_oil_crisis
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

	}
	option = { #borghese
		name = coupdebug.1.b
		ITA_army_add_borghese_pop = yes
		ITA_navy_add_borghese_pop = yes
		ITA_airforce_add_borghese_pop = yes
		ITA_carabinieri_add_borghese_pop = yes
		set_global_flag = ITA_lost_oil_crisis
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

	}
}

#end of insurrection in Kenya
country_event = {
	id = ita.105
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.105"}
	title = ita.105.t
	desc = ita.105.d

	trigger = {
		AND = {
			tag = ITA
			date > 1962.07.18
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = ita.105.a
		add_political_power = 25
		547 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 2
			}
			damage_building = {
				type = offices
				damage = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = itafirstelection.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event itafirstelection.1"}
	title = itafirstelection.1.t
	desc = itafirstelection.1.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = itafirstelection.1.a
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = -20
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = socialist
			long_name = ITA_socialist_first_party_long
			name = ITA_socialist_first_party
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_x_mas

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #The delegates vote infavor of Il Duce
		name = vc.18.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = ita_ciano_clout
				value = ita_scorza_clout
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}

		country_event = { id = vc.19 days = 1 }

		clear_variable = ita_ciano_clout
		clear_variable = ita_scorza_clout
	}

	option = { #The delegates vote against Il Duce
		name = vc.18.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { ita_ciano_clout < ita_scorza_clout }
		}

		country_event = { id = vc.20 days = 1 }

		clear_variable = ita_ciano_clout
		clear_variable = ita_scorza_clout
	}
}

					}
				}

		}
	}
}

			last_election = "1970.4.28"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
			ruling_party = liberal_democracy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = german_civil_war_goeringvic
				}
			}
			load_focus_tree = ita_cd_1970
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = german_civil_war_goeringvic
			}
			load_focus_tree = ita_cd_1970_goering
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ITA_PIANO_SOLO_COUP
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_legacy_of_PS_tt
			multiply_variable = {
				var = ITA_RIGHT_EXTREMISM_PS
				value = -1
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = ITA_LEFT_EXTREMISM_PS
				value = -1
			}
			clr_country_flag = ITA_PIANO_SOLO_COUP

			set_variable = {
				var = ITA_i_give_up_piano_solo_is_boolean_now
				value = 0
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_country_fucked_by_riots }
		}
	}
}

## FANFANI GANG TERRITORY ##

country_event = {
	id = christdem.51 # Fanfani enters office
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event christdem.51"}
	title = christdem.51.t
	desc = christdem.51.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_left_wing_students
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = christdem.51.a
		load_focus_tree = ita_cd_1970
		set_country_flag = ITA_YOL_begun
		custom_effect_tooltip = "You will unlock counter terror decisions."
		clamp_variable = {
			var = ITA_political
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = ITA_media
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = ITA_corporations
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = ITA_faith_in_gov
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalArmy > ITA_Sogno_RoyalArmy }
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = ITA_army
				value = 0.25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalNavy > ITA_Sogno_RoyalNavy }
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = ITA_army
				value = 0.25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalAirforce > ITA_Sogno_RoyalAirforce }
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = ITA_army
				value = 0.25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_Carabinieri > ITA_Borghese_Carabinieri }
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = ITA_army
				value = 0.25
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = nscorza.100
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nscorza.100"}

			TNO_worsen_trade_unions_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
		}
		else = {
			TNO_improve_trade_unions_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Silence, Sogno disappears
	id = scorzaseventies.9
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event scorzaseventies.9"}
	title = scorzaseventies.9.t
	desc = scorzaseventies.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_left_wing_students

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # oh well
		name = scorzaseventies.9.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = ITA_Borghese_RoyalArmy
						value = ITA_Sogno_RoyalArmy
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = ITA_Coup_Ability
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = ITA_Borghese_RoyalNavy
						value = ITA_Sogno_RoyalNavy
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = ITA_Coup_Ability
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = ITA_Borghese_RoyalAirforce
						value = ITA_Sogno_RoyalAirforce
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = ITA_Coup_Ability
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = ITA_Borghese_Blackshirts
						value = ITA_Sogno_Blackshirts
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = ITA_Coup_Ability
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = ITA_Borghese_Carabinieri
						value = ITA_Sogno_Carabinieri
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = ITA_Coup_Ability
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = ITA_Coup_Ability
						value = 3
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = scorzaseventies.10 days = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = ITA_Coup_Ability
							value = 3
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = scorzaseventies.11 days = 12 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Crackdown in the colonies
	id = scorza.12
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event scorza.12"}
	title = scorza.12.t
	desc = scorza.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_right_wing_students1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = scorza.12.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_restoring_control_scorza
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ITA_nationwide_protests4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ITA_nationwide_protests4
					add_idea = ITA_nationwide_protests3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ITA_nationwide_protests3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ITA_nationwide_protests3
					add_idea = ITA_nationwide_protests2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ITA_nationwide_protests2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ITA_nationwide_protests2
					add_idea = ITA_nationwide_protests1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ITA_nationwide_protests1
				}
				remove_ideas = ITA_nationwide_protests1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #core suez
	id = demitaly.36
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event demitaly.36"}
	title = demitaly.36.t
	desc = demitaly.36.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_x_mas

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = demitaly.36.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = ita_suez_colonization_points
						value = 4
						compare = greater_than
					}
				}
				ITA = {
					transfer_state = 965
					add_state_core = 965
					transfer_state = 1160
					add_state_core = 1160
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = ita_suez_colonization_points
						value = 4
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				EGY = {
					remove_state_core = 965
					remove_state_claim = 965
					remove_state_core = 1160
					remove_state_claim = 1160
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = blocchinazionale

country_event = { #BN wins
	id = blocchinazionale.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event blocchinazionale.1"}
	title = blocchinazionale.1.t
	desc = blocchinazionale.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty1


	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = blocchinazionale.1.a
		load_focus_tree = ita_conservative_democracy_victory
		set_politics = {
			last_election = "1966.4.28"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democracy
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = itapartyunity.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event itapartyunity.1"}
	title = itapartyunity.1.t
	desc = itapartyunity.1.d
	hidden = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_right_rally
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = itapartyunity.1.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ITA
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ITA_FD_colapse
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ITA_BN_colapse
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = itapartyunity.1
				days = 7
				random = 0
			}
		}
		clear_variable = ITA_BN_Strength
		clear_variable = ITA_FD_Strength
		ITA_stability_update = yes
		ITA_wing_unity_FD = yes
		ITA_wing_unity_BN = yes
		ITA_FD_popularity = yes
		ITA_BN_popularity = yes
		ITA_CD_popularity = yes
		ITA_Party_Die_CheckFD = yes
		ITA_Party_Die_CheckBN = yes

		set_temp_variable = { ITA_FD_life = 0 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { ITA_FD_life = ITA_FDDivide }
		add_to_temp_variable = { ITA_FD_life = ita_stability_drag }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { ITA_FD_life = ita_FD_unity }

		set_temp_variable = { ITA_BN_life = 0 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { ITA_BN_life = ITA_BNDivide }
		add_to_temp_variable = { ITA_BN_life = ita_stability_drag }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { ITA_BN_life = ita_BN_unity }

		set_variable = {
			var = ITA_BN_Strength
			value = ITA_BN_life
		}

		set_variable = {
			var = ITA_FD_Strength
			value = ITA_FD_life
		}
	}
}

country_event = { ## FD DIES, Natural
	id = itapartyunity.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event itapartyunity.5"}
	title = itapartyunity.5.t
	desc = itapartyunity.5.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = itapartyunity.5.a
		set_country_flag = ITA_FD_colapse
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = socialist
			long_name = ITA_communist_party_dem_long
			name = ITA_communist_party_dem
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_democracy
			long_name = ITA_socialist_first_party
			name = ITA_socialist_first_party
		}
		set_temp_variable = { BNBoys = party_popularity@authoritarian_democracy }
		add_to_temp_variable = { BNBoys = party_popularity@fascism }
		add_to_temp_variable = { BNFBoys = party_popularity@despotism }
		set_temp_variable = { FDBoys = party_popularity@socialist }
		add_to_temp_variable = { FDBoys = party_popularity@social_democracy }
		set_temp_variable = { CDBoys = party_popularity@liberal_democracy }
		add_to_temp_variable = { CDBoys = party_popularity@conservative_democracy }
		set_variable = { BNCheck = BNBoys }
		set_variable = { FDCheck = FDBoys }
		set_variable = { CDCheck = CDBoys }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = socialist
					has_government = social_democracy
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ita_1970_elections
				}
			}
			add_stability = -0.2
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = FDCheck
						value = BNCheck
						compare = less_than
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = FDCheck
							value = CDCheck
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
				}
				load_focus_tree = ita_FD_to_BN_1966
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = FDCheck
						value = CDCheck
						compare = less_than
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = FDCheck
							value = BNCheck
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
				}
				load_focus_tree = ita_FD_to_CD_1966
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = FDCheck
						value = CDCheck
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = FDCheck
						value = BNCheck
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = CDCheck
							value = BNCheck
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
					load_focus_tree = ita_FD_to_BN_1966
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = FDCheck
							value = CDCheck
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
					load_focus_tree = ita_FD_to_CD_1966
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = FDCheck
							value = CDCheck
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
							load_focus_tree = ita_FD_to_BN_1966
						}
						50 = {
							load_focus_tree = ita_FD_to_CD_1966
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

	id = ITAOIL.103
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ITAOIL.103"}
	title = ITAOIL.103.t
	desc = ITAOIL.103.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_blackshirts1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	option = {
		name = ITAOIL.103.a
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = ITA_run_the_propaganda_fatigue
			value = 1
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = ITA_run_the_propaganda_fatigue
			min = 0
			max = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_run_the_propaganda_fatigue > 0 }
				has_country_flag = ITA_oil_crisis_demitaly_war
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ITAOIL.103
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #All In Saudi Coup
	id = ITAOIL.505
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ITAOIL.505"}
	title = ITAOIL.505.t
	desc = ITAOIL.505.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_right_rally
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ITAOIL.505.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ITAOIL.506 days = 1 }
			SAU = {
				country_event = { id = ITAOIL.507 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ITAOIL.505.b
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ITA_talal_coup
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = ITA_talal_coup
					value = 3
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ITAOIL.508 days = 1 }
				SAU = {
					country_event = { id = ITAOIL.509 days = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = ITA_talal_coup
					value = 3
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ITAOIL.506 days = 1 }
				SAU = {
					country_event = { id = ITAOIL.507 days = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ITAOIL.505.c
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ITAOIL.506 days = 1 }
			SAU = {
				country_event = { id = ITAOIL.507 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = saragat.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event saragat.1"}
	title = saragat.1.t
	desc = saragat.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_saragat2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = saragat.1.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = german_civil_war_goeringvic
				}
			}
			load_focus_tree = ita_1970_FD
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = german_civil_war_goeringvic
			}
			load_focus_tree = ita_1970_FD_goering
		}
		promote_character = ITA_Giuseppe_Saragat
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democracy
			last_election = "1966.6.23"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democracy
			popularity = .1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ITA_PIANO_SOLO_COUP
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_legacy_of_PS_tt
			multiply_variable = {
				var = ITA_RIGHT_EXTREMISM_PS
				value = -1
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = ITA_LEFT_EXTREMISM_PS
				value = -1
			}
			clr_country_flag = ITA_PIANO_SOLO_COUP

			multiply_variable = {
				var = ITA_i_give_up_piano_solo_is_boolean_now
				value = 0
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_country_fucked_by_riots }
		}
	}
}

			max = 1

country_event = {
	id = marsanich.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event marsanich.1"}
	title = marsanich.1.t
	desc = marsanich.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_right_wing_students2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = marsanich.1.a
		promote_character = ITA_Achille_Lauro
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democracy
			last_election = "1966.6.23"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democracy
			popularity = .1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = german_civil_war_goeringvic
				}
			}
			load_focus_tree = ita_bn_1970
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = german_civil_war_goeringvic
			}
			load_focus_tree = ita_bn_1970_goering
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ITA_PIANO_SOLO_COUP
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_legacy_of_PS_tt
			multiply_variable = {
				var = ITA_RIGHT_EXTREMISM_PS
				value = -1
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = ITA_LEFT_EXTREMISM_PS
				value = -1
			}
			clr_country_flag = ITA_PIANO_SOLO_COUP

			set_variable = {
				var = ITA_i_give_up_piano_solo_is_boolean_now
				value = 0
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_country_fucked_by_riots }
		}
	}
}

		name = marsanich.2.a
		set_country_flag = ITA_YOL_begun
		custom_effect_tooltip = "You will unlock counter terror decisions."
		clamp_variable = {
			var = ITA_political
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = ITA_media
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = ITA_corporations
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = ITA_faith_in_gov
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalArmy > ITA_Sogno_RoyalArmy }
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = ITA_army
				value = 0.25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalNavy > ITA_Sogno_RoyalNavy }
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = ITA_army
				value = 0.25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalAirforce > ITA_Sogno_RoyalAirforce }
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = ITA_army
				value = 0.25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_Carabinieri > ITA_Borghese_Carabinieri }
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = ITA_army

			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event FD.1"}
	title = FD.1.t
	desc = FD.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_right_wing_students1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # SocDem
		name = FD.1.a
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
							rule = ITA_FD_socdem_or_libsoc
							option = ITA_FD_ROUTE_LIBSOC_DEMOCRATIC
					}
					has_game_rule = {
							rule = ITA_FD_socdem_or_libsoc
							option = ITA_FD_ROUTE_LIBSOC_COUP
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = socialist
				popularity = -0.11
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democracy
				popularity = -0.33
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = socialist
				popularity = 0.11
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democracy
				popularity = 0.33
			}
			complete_national_focus = ita_prima_la_democrazia
			set_country_flag = ITA_FD_socdem
		}

	}
	option = { # LibSoc
		name = FD.1.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
							rule = ITA_FD_socdem_or_libsoc
							option = ITA_FD_ROUTE_SOCDEM_LEFT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
							rule = ITA_FD_socdem_or_libsoc
							option = ITA_FD_ROUTE_SOCDEM_CENTER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = socialist
				popularity = -0.11
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democracy
				popularity = -0.33
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = socialist
				popularity = 0.33
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democracy
				popularity = 0.11
			}
			complete_national_focus = ita_prima_il_socialismo
		}
		set_country_flag = ITA_FD_libsoc
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = { #implemented
			ITA_Enrico_Berlinguer_hog
			ITA_Giorgio_Amendola_sec
			ITA_Sandro_Pertini_for
			ITA_Riccardio_Lombardi_eco
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = socialist
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ITA_Pietro_Nenni = {
				promote_character = {
    					ideology = socialist_revolutionary_frontism_subtype
  				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			MNT = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ITA
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			ALB = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ITA
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			TUN = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ITA
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			LBA = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ITA
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				if = { # good boy
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = ita_good_boy_points
							value = ita_bad_boy_points
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						news_event = {
							id = WORLD.955
							days = 1
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = { # bad boy
					limit = {
					}
					every_country = {
						news_event = {
							id = WORLD.955
							days = 1
						}
					}
				}
				# come back here poopyshit
			}
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = borghese
country_event = { #Borghese Coup
	id = borghese.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event borghese.1"}
	title = borghese.1.t
	desc = borghese.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_left_wing_students

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_global_flag = ITA_lost_oil_crisis
			count_triggers = {
				amount = 4
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalArmy > ITA_Sogno_RoyalArmy }
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalNavy > ITA_Sogno_RoyalNavy }
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalAirforce > ITA_Sogno_RoyalAirforce }
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_Blackshirts > ITA_Sogno_Blackshirts }
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_Carabinieri > ITA_Borghese_Carabinieri }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #
		name = borghese.1.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
		}
		retire_country_leader = yes
		promote_character = ITA_Junio_Valerio_Borghese
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			set_country_flag = TNO_closing_screen_show
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = sogno

country_event = { #Sogno Coup
	id = sogno.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sogno.1"}
	title = sogno.1.t
	desc = sogno.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_right_rally

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_global_flag = ITA_lost_oil_crisis
			has_country_leader = { character = ITA_Carlo_Scorza ruling_only = yes }
			count_triggers = {
				amount = 4
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalArmy < ITA_Sogno_RoyalArmy }
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalNavy < ITA_Sogno_RoyalNavy }
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_RoyalAirforce < ITA_Sogno_RoyalAirforce }
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_Blackshirts < ITA_Sogno_Blackshirts }
				check_variable = { ITA_Borghese_Carabinieri < ITA_Borghese_Carabinieri }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #
		name = sogno.1.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = despotism
		}
		promote_character = ITA_Edgardo_Sogno
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			set_country_flag = TNO_closing_screen_show
		}
	}
}

###Göring - Italy Great Game Events###

country_event = { #Hungary Defended
	id = ita.5000
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.5000"}
	title = ita.5000.t
	desc = ita.5000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_election

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = ita.5000.a
		add_command_power = 50
		add_political_power = 300
		army_experience = 200
		puppet = HUN
		hidden_effect = {
			HUN = {
				retire_country_leader = yes
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				set_popularities = {
					social_democracy = 7
					liberal_democracy = 13
					conservative_democracy = 21
					authoritarian_democracy = 36
					communist = 10
					socialist = 13
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = empiremanagement.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event empiremanagement.2"}
	title = empiremanagement.2.t
	desc = empiremanagement.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_right_wing_students2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # set nothing
		name = empiremanagement.2.a
		ITA_egypt_points_0 = yes
	}
	option = { # set 1
		name = empiremanagement.2.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = ITA_empire_management_coins
				value = 1
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		ITA_egypt_points_1 = yes
	}
	option = { # set 2
		name = empiremanagement.2.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = ITA_empire_management_coins
				value = 2
				compare = greater_than_or_equals

		}

add_namespace = empiremanagement_egypt

country_event = { # Farouk dies, how much do we commit?
	id = empiremanagement_egypt.1
	title = empiremanagement_egypt.1.t
	desc = empiremanagement_egypt.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_right_rally


	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event empiremanagement_egypt.1" }

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # set nothing
		name = empiremanagement_egypt.1.a
		ITA_egypt_points_0 = yes
		# random
	}
	option = { # set 1
		name = empiremanagement_egypt.1.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = ITA_empire_management_coins
				value = 1
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		ITA_egypt_points_1 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.05 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		EGY = {
			TNO_improve_admin_efficiency_low = yes
		}
		# random, lean adalberto
	}
	option = { # set 2
		name = empiremanagement_egypt.1.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = ITA_empire_management_coins
				value = 2
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		ITA_egypt_points_2 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.05 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		add_manpower = -2000
		EGY = {
			add_manpower = 2000
			TNO_improve_admin_efficiency_med = yes
		}
		# random, lean adalberto or moniem
	}
	option = { # set 3
		name = empiremanagement_egypt.1.d
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = ITA_empire_management_coins
				value = 3
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		ITA_egypt_points_3 = yes
		# choice: adalberto, republic, or moniem
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.1 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		add_manpower = -2000
		EGY = {
			add_manpower = 2000
			TNO_improve_admin_efficiency_med = yes
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Choose a new leader
	id = empiremanagement_egypt.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event empiremanagement_egypt.2"}
	title = empiremanagement_egypt.2.t
	desc = empiremanagement_egypt.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # moniem
		name = empiremanagement_egypt.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
		}
		modifier = {
		    factor = 0
			has_game_rule = { rule = EGY_PATH option =  EGY_PATH_COLONIAL }
		}
		
		modifier = {
		    factor = 0
			has_game_rule = { rule = EGY_PATH option =  EGY_PATH_AD }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			EGY = {
				retire_character = EGY_Farouk_I
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = EGY_Muhammad_Abdel_Moneim
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						expire = "2018.01.01"
						ideology = despotism_aristocratic_conservatism_subtype
						id = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.912
					days = 1
				}
				ITA = {
					country_event = { id = empiremanagement_egypt.4 days = 365 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # republic
		name = empiremanagement_egypt.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		modifier = {
		    factor = 0
			has_game_rule = { rule = EGY_PATH option =  EGY_PATH_COLONIAL }
		}
		
		modifier = {
		    factor = 0
			has_game_rule = { rule = EGY_PATH option =  EGY_PATH_DESPOTISM }
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			EGY = {
				retire_character = EGY_Farouk_I
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = EGY_Anwar_Sadat
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						expire = "2018.01.01"
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy_provisional_government_subtype
						id = -1
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				set_popularities = {
					social_democracy = 9
					liberal_democracy = 7
					conservative_democracy = 11
					authoritarian_democracy = 43
					communist = 21
					socialist = 9
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.911
					days = 1
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				country_event = { id = empiremanagement_egypt.5 days = 365 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # adalberto
		name = empiremanagement_egypt.2.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		modifier = {
		    factor = 0
			has_game_rule = { rule = EGY_PATH option =  EGY_PATH_DESPOTISM }
		}
		
		modifier = {
		    factor = 0
			has_game_rule = { rule = EGY_PATH option =  EGY_PATH_AD }
		}
		
		EGY = {
			retire_character = EGY_Farouk_I
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = EGY_Adalberto_Genova
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					expire = "2018.01.01"
					ideology = despotism_colonial_government_subtype
					id = -1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.913
					days = 1
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				country_event = { id = empiremanagement_egypt.3 days = 365 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Adalberto special event
	id = empiremanagement_egypt.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event empiremanagement_egypt.3"}
	title = empiremanagement_egypt.3.t
	desc = empiremanagement_egypt.3.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_italy_right_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # set nothing
		name = empiremanagement_egypt.3.a
		ITA_egypt_points_0 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = empiremanagement_egypt.6 days = 250 }
		}
	}
	option = { # set 1
		name = empiremanagement_egypt.3.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = ITA_empire_management_coins
				value = 1
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = EGY_oil_crisis_defense_int
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = empiremanagement_egypt.6 days = 250 }
		}
		ITA_egypt_points_1 = yes
	}
	option = { # set 2
		name = empiremanagement_egypt.3.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = ITA_empire_management_coins
				value = 2
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = EGY_oil_crisis_defense_int
			value = 2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = empiremanagement_egypt.6 days = 250 }
		}
		ITA_egypt_points_2 = yes
	}
	option = { # set 3
		name = empiremanagement_egypt.3.d
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = ITA_empire_management_coins
				value = 3
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = EGY_oil_crisis_defense_int
			value = 3
		}

		}

	}

			name = ITA_IRQ_benefeit
			value = 3
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			gdp_growth_temp  = 0.004
		}
		econ_gdp_growth_change  = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRQ_MONEY_IN_IRQ
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = ITA_IRQ_benefeit
						value = 6
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = empiremanagement_IRQ.7 days = 160 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # set nothing
		name = empiremanagement_ILG.4.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				ITA = {
					check_variable = {
						var = ITA_ILG_benefeit
						value = 5
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				country_event = { id = empiremanagement_ILG.5 days = 12 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ITA = {
					check_variable = {
						var = ITA_ILG_benefeit
						value = 5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				country_event = { id = empiremanagement_ILG.6 days = 12 }
			}
		}
	}
}
